***pearly.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pearly.html>pearly</a> (59660)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pearl.html>pearl</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pearly.html>pearly</a></strong> (<i>countable <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pearlies</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncommon<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pale.html>pale</a> greyish <a href = vnd.unilang:white.html>white</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:colour.html>colour</a>, tinted <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blue.html>blue</a>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:pech.html>Pech</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:bad.html>bad</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:luck.html>luck</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:pitch.html>pitch</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:tar.html>tar</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:high.html>High</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">peh</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pīx</i>. <p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">pekker</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:peck.html>peck</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pick.html>pick</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:something.html>something</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:manner.html>manner</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bird.html>bird</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">forming <a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a> nouns</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***pendelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pendelen.html>pendelen</a> (43235)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">pendeln</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pendulum</i>; <a href = vnd.unilang:ultimately.html>ultimately</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pendulus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hanging</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
